# The Kindilar were one of several related tribes that mass migrated into the Rây
# Despite being one of a dozen or so tribes, their name stuck as the blanket term for the dune sea tribesmen now adapting to life in the Rây
# Bellakar had trouble in Mardruak and was unable to support their allies, until the council of regent was restored some 200 years later
# by Juke

#####################
### Adyara Clans  ###
#####################
# Coven-Tribes in the Dune Sea
# Tribes founded by a legendary witch in the dune sea, few things are known about her, most very vague.

# stolen from her tribe during a raid, wed forcibly, Went to mordor with her husband, learned sorcery there, eventually sent back to the dune sea as an agent of sauron
# The 'Tale of the Witch and the Spider' tells of her origins - she was a peasant girl who was kidnapped by a black numenorean and forcibly wed at a young age, taken to mordor. Her husband was poisoned either by her or in the politics of mordor.
# Learned dark rituals in mordor, returned and spread her teachings to the surrounding tribes, founding the cult of Sanbaiz, the great spider
# Identity of Sanbaiz deliberately vague, should be interpreted as sauron but  also as a reference to Shelob

lineadara0 = {	#legendary dune sea clanmother, rumored sorceress, several tribes claim descent from her
	name = Adya
	female = yes
	dynasty = dynasty_adyara

	religion = faith_sanbaiz
	culture = sand_people 

	trait = beauty_good_3
	trait = shrewd
	trait = fecund
	trait = sorcerer_1
	trait = witch
	trait = schemer
	trait = torturer
	trait = seducer
	trait = theologian
	trait = scholar
	
	trait = deceitful
	trait = patient
	trait = callous

	diplomacy = 8
	martial = 9
	stewardship = 6
	intrigue = 9
	learning = 8
	prowess = 9

	trait = education_intrigue_4

	6674.3.11 = {
		birth = yes
	}
	
	6720.1.1 = {
		give_nickname = nick_mother_of_shades
		effect = {
			add_character_flag = {
				flag = had_nickname_event
			}
		}
	}

		death = { death_reason = death_vanished }
	}

#DentedEar Note: The Near-future of the central Dune Sea
#
#It is a time of upheaval in the central Dune Sea. Two generations ago, Ozren "the Holy" successfully
#is not the only faith to have found a champion. popularised the faith of Gurzil at the oasis of Jetin.
#However his family is on the decline, and his is not the only faith to have found it's champion.The
#[REDACTED], who associate Gurzil with Vatra, the great enemy, are on the rise. Taking advantege of the 
#collapse of the Peduages dynasty, [REDACTED] would sieze power for himself. He would send his warriors
#forth to battle against the Ozrenes in a rage of zealous fury, wiping them off of the face of the world.
#This would cause a mass Gurzilite exodous into Narak, fleeing from [REDACTED]'s ire, which would give
#rise to the Jelut people who would later go on to conquer Umbar. But in time, the [REDACTED] rule over
#the Dune Sea too would come to an end. They would flee to the south-western highlands, seeking [REDACTED] 
#protection from those they had once ruled, and leaving the central Dune Sea once more to Shasmekh alone.
#
#([REDACTED] being important totally isn't an excuse for me to not continue to the Kinstrife right now.)

### HOUSE OF PEDUAG ###
#######################
